msg:Three days before Labor Day, I suddenly got excited and asked two adults to go to Wuxi together. My husband suddenly saw this hotel with villa-style rooms and wanted to take his parents to experience it, so he quickly booked 3 rooms for 3 days and 2 nights.
[Communication before check-in] Because I was traveling with my parents, I was used to contacting the hotel in advance and asked them to reserve 3 adjacent rooms. At the same time, I asked about the extra bed. The hotel confirmed the demand very smoothly.
[Butler service] Before check-in, I added the butler WeChat in advance. The butler Lasa provided us with services throughout the whole process. Thank you very much. The butler responded very quickly and the meticulous service made us feel very good throughout the trip.
[Extra bed] It is worth mentioning that their extra bed service is very reasonable, 500 per night, but it includes a breakfast. The extra bed can be placed on the first floor, and there is enough space.
[Breakfast] My family basically travels together around 7:30 for breakfast. There are not many people in the restaurant. Although there are not many choices, the noodles and wontons are freshly cooked, and there are many choices of toppings. The taste is very good.
[Accommodation] It's quite cool in this season, and there are not many bugs, but the main thing is to remember to close the door or pull the screen window after checking in, otherwise there will definitely be bugs on the first floor running in. Mosquito repellent will be provided, and it is also very convenient to replace it after use. The room is very spacious, and there are toilets and showers upstairs and downstairs, which is quite convenient. L'Occitane's toiletries.
[Service] In fact, the scenery of the entire park is very garden-like, but it is slightly lacking in maintenance. I originally thought that there were fewer people on Labor Day, which lowered the expectations of hotel services. After all, we have to understand the peak period. As a result, whether it is the shuttle bus for travel or the room cleaning, the hotel staff serve with a friendly smile. When it rains, they will help to park under the eaves. It's really thoughtful. When traveling to Sunac Mall, they can also deliver to the nearest door, and they will also inform the description of the return pick-up point, which is very convenient.
[Special services] They have a small boat experience, which is very good. Because there are not many people and boats, you need to make an appoin**ent with the housekeeper in advance. You can choose to deliver from the lobby to the room, or you can choose to make an appoin**ent to pick up in the room and deliver to the lobby. It's a very interesting experience. The big sister who runs the boat is also very kind.
[Off topic] Actually, before this trip, I read a lot of bad reviews on Xiaohongshu, Dianping, and Ctrip, and I was a little hesitant, but after the actual trip, I really felt that it was not as bad as they said, especially the hotel service. The brothers and uncles who helped us send us were all very kind and thoughtful. Thank you very much! 
So I will write a long article to describe my real personal experience for your reference.

msg:I often come to Wuxi, but this is the first time I brought my family to Xuelang Songpin Hotel. I experienced the feeling of staying in a two-bedroom lake view villa and a one-bedroom river view villa for three nights and four days. Both the two-bedroom lake view house and the one-bedroom river view house are two-story Hui-style courtyard villas. Flowers and plants are planted inside and outside the courtyard, and are arranged at random with rockeries. You can also enjoy the red and white plum blossoms that are still in bloom. , it‚Äôs really pleasing to the eye. The living room in the room is high and spacious, and the Chinese style is both luxurious and comfortable; the bedroom is clean and bright, fully equipped, quiet and comfortable. The back doors and windows of the two villas face the river. Whether you stand in front of the window, or go out and stand on the riverside platform or the steps of the river port, the clear river water flows slowly before your eyes. The hotel is large in scale, with lakes, rivers, pavilions, flowers and trees scattered among it, and together with the Anhui-style buildings including the lobby and guest rooms, it forms an exquisite and beautiful large-scale garden. The only shortcoming is that there are some deficiencies in management. A few dead and collapsed bamboos and trees have not been dealt with, and some damaged scenic spots, facilities and trails have not been repaired in time, which affects the overall appearance.
      The service attitude of the hotel staff is commendable. Whether it is the butler-style service of the reception staff at the front desk, the cleaning service of the room cleaner Miao Fengni, or the pick-up and meal delivery services of the battery car driver Li Youtao, they are all very enthusiastic and meticulous towards our elderly guests. The thoughtfulness made us feel warm.

msg:I‚Äôve always wanted to go to Wuxi to see the cherry blossoms. I‚Äôm very busy at work, so it‚Äôs hard to find time to take time off and come to Wuxi this year. In order to avoid unnecessary distractions, I chose the most expensive hotel in Wuxi - Wuxi Xuelang Songpin Hotel. I thought it was a beautiful meditation trip, but I didn't expect it to become a nightmare.
1. Inconsistent service promises: I found on the Internet that the hotel can take a boat to the room. Before booking, I called the front desk to confirm that "you can contact the housekeeper at any time to take photos with the boat when you are not busy." However, after checking in, the front desk informed that the boat can be used once. Once you use it, you can't borrow it again. It feels like you've been defrauded, but it doesn't hurt. At worst, you don't want to take the boat to check in and take pictures later, so I choose to take the battery car to the room.
2. Damage to the guest's finances: It was precisely because of the inconsistency at the front desk (or perhaps out of fear of trouble) that I chose to take a battery car to the room. The hotel damaged my 10,000-yuan suitcase. This suitcase was purchased during the epidemic and was basically basic after purchase. I didn't leave Beijing, so I didn't use it at all, and when I used it this time, I was careful and it was basically as good as new. However, the hotel's battery cart did not take safety into account when transporting luggage and guests. It made a sharp turn and threw my box more than ten meters away, causing the front of the box to fall. Multiple injuries.
3. Threatening customers to challenge the bottom line: Regarding the financial damage, there was a female manager on duty at first, who had a very good attitude, although she did not give a good handling method. Then she changed to a man, who told me that the claim settlement time would be long and made me give up. This idea immediately angered me. I asked which insurance company it was from, but they were still unwilling to provide it. Later, a so-called marketing manager, Ms. Jiang Xiaoyan, said righteously that she had used my personal information and the box‚Äôs ID code to check the purchase record of the box without authorization. I had bought the box for more than two years, and who knew who caused the wear and tear, which angered me again.
4. Not active in refunding: The case of the box was finally settled, and Ctrip intervened and compensated more than 1,000 yuan. If this attitude and rhetoric had not been used earlier, we would not have had any trouble in Wuxi. unhappy.
5. Room hygiene issues: For a room fee of more than 2,600 yuan, there are leftover snacks from the previous guest in the room, hair on the bed, and an unknown black substance in the bathtub. The hygiene conditions are not as good as those of an express hotel worth several hundred yuan.
6. Hotel safety hazards: The price of a lake view room is twice that of a river view room. However, the so-called lake view is artificial water that has not been taken care of for a long time, not Taihu Lake, and the plank roads by the lake are all damaged. If children are not taken care of, Running around is a huge safety hazard.
7. Other service issues: Before checking in, I consulted with the hotel about the free travel photos included in the package. The ******* who answered the phone insisted that our package did not include travel photos, which caused us to waste time repeatedly confirming with Ctrip. In fact, the package included it, and we didn‚Äôt know what the front desk said. Why did the lady do this? She set out to take pictures at 6:30 in the morning and asked the hotel to deliver breakfast to the room at 6:10. She thought that at least there would be hot porridge or eggs, but the meal price of more than 500 yuan only gave two breads and a bag of yogurt. , simply unable to support the physical strength of playing in the scenic spot for half a day, and a customer butler named Tom kept telling you that breakfast will not be served until 6:30, which is good, and the next day we changed hotels due to disputes (only Xuelang Song (Half the price of hotel tasting), departure at 5:00 in the morning, the hotel sent bread, donuts, yogurt, eggs, some fruits, and also expressed its apology.
8. If the experience is poor, it is the customer's problem: I stayed at Wuxi Xuelang Songpin Hotel for a total of 14 hours. Apart from sleeping and eating out, I was just defending my rights. I didn't really experience the hotel, let alone the more than 500 yuan for breakfast, check-in or check-in for two in the package. Check-out cruise experience, etc., but the other party emphasized that we did not ask to change rooms ourselves. Although they did not take the initiative to change rooms for us, the hotel would change us if we did. If we did not mention it, it is the customer's fault. To this day, there is only compensation for the financial damage, but no compensation for the problems caused by the room and service.
It‚Äôs hard to imagine that this is the most expensive hotel in Wuxi. The most expensive really doesn‚Äôt mean the best, or even good. Please stay safe.
